<content full_path="README.md">
# aztec-state-migration

## Test

Note: It test migration from and to the same aztec network. TODO: configure setup with 2 aztec networks deployed on the same L1.

1. 
```sh
# install dependencies
yarn install
yarn sol:deps
# compile contracts
yarn noir:compile
yarn sol:compile
# generate noir contract ts artifacts
yarn noir:codegen
```
2.
```sh
# start local aztec rollups (on anvil)
yarn test:setup
```

3.
```sh
# run the test
yarn test:migration
```

4.
```sh
# stop the rollups
yarn test:stop
```

</content>

<content full_path="CLAUDE.md">
# CLAUDE.md — Dual-Rollup Migration (Aztec + Noir)

## 0) Definitions (read once)
- Noir: A programming language for zero-knowledge proofs (proofs that show something is true without revealing secret data).
- Aztec: A zkRollup (a Layer 2 network that uses zero-knowledge proofs).
- L1 (Layer 1): The base chain (usually Ethereum).
- L2 (Layer 2): A chain that settles to L1.
- MCP (Model Context Protocol): A local tool interface Claude can use to search and read code/doc repos.
- TDD (test-driven development): Write a failing test first, then write the smallest code to pass it.

---

# SECTION A — PROJECT-SPECIFIC RULES (do not skip)

## A1) Tech stack and versions (source of truth)
- Noir: `v1.0.0-beta.x`
- Aztec Network: `v3.0.0-devnet.6-patch.1`
- Build tool: Nargo (Noir CLI + package tool)
- TypeScript tooling: Yarn scripts (see A3)
- Solidity: Present in this repo (exact compiler/version must be taken from repo config, not guessed)

**Rules**
1) Never guess versions. Read them from:
   - `package.json` / lockfile
   - `Nargo.toml`
   - any Solidity config present (`foundry.toml`, `hardhat.config.*`, `remappings.txt`, etc.)
2) When Aztec APIs are involved, prefer local code in `node_modules/@aztec/` over online docs.

## A2) Project docs and architecture (source of truth)
### Purpose
This repo implements a **dual-rollup migration** using cryptographic proofs anchored by L1.

### Spec and architecture files (standard layout)
We keep docs in `docs/` using a layout that can be reused across projects.

**Spec (migration design including Mode A / Mode B)**
- `docs/spec/migration-spec.md`  ← high level specification

**Architecture**
- `docs/arch/overview.md`        ← dual-rollup architecture summary
- `docs/arch/flows.md`           ← step-by-step flows (Mode A / Mode B)
- `docs/arch/threat-model.md`    ← trust assumptions + threat model

**Operational docs**
- `docs/ops/testing.md`          ← how to run tests locally and in CI
- `docs/ops/deploy.md`           ← if deploy exists in this repo
- `docs/ops/troubleshooting.md`  ← common local network issues

**Change log (mandatory for every code change)**
- `docs/DEVLOG.md`

**Rules**
1) Any time you need "how Aztec works" or "standard library details," check the local `node_modules/@aztec/` implementation first.
2) Treat `node_modules/@aztec/` as **read-only** unless the task explicitly asks to change it.
3) If you rename or move doc files, update references in `README.md` and any internal links.

## A3) Local development commands (use these exact commands unless repo scripts change)

### Compilation
- Noir compile: `yarn noir:compile`
- TypeScript bindings/codegen: `yarn noir:codegen`
- Solidity compile: `yarn sol:compile`
- Clean: `yarn clean`

### Testing

### Recommended verification defaults
- Fast checks (default): `yarn check:fast`
- Full E2E (only when needed): `yarn check:full`

Use `yarn check:full` when changes affect:
- migration flow logic across old/new rollup
- archive root verification
- L1↔L2 message consumption
- note hashing / nullifier behavior that the E2E test exercises

- Unit tests (Noir): `nargo test --show-output`

### E2E migration test (complex flow)
1) Setup (starts dual rollup sandboxes):
   - `yarn test:setup`  
   - OLD sandbox: `http://localhost:8080`
   - NEW sandbox: `http://localhost:8081`
2) Run migration test:
   - `yarn test:migration`
3) Stop and clean up:
   - `yarn test:stop`

**Rules**
1) When you change migration logic, run the E2E test flow unless it is impossible (then explain exactly why).
2) If you change ports, endpoints, or scripts, update:
   - `README.md`
   - `docs/ops/testing.md`
   - and `docs/DEVLOG.md`

## A4) “No guessing” rule for Aztec standard library and helpers
- If the task references “standard library,” “aztec-nr,” or a helper function:
  1) Use Aztec plugin MCP search to locate the real implementation in `node_modules/@aztec/`.
  2) Quote file paths and function names from the local repo.
  3) Only use online docs if local code does not answer the question.

---

# SECTION B — GENERAL OPERATING RULES (edit only if workflow changes)

## B1) Installed plugins and routing

### 1) Superpowers (obra/superpowers) — use for HOW we work
Use it for workflow discipline:
- Brainstorm (only if requirements are unclear)
- Plan
- TDD implementation (tests first where practical)
- Verify (run commands)
- Review (read diff for correctness and style)

### 2) Aztec plugin (critesjosh/aztec-claude-plugin) — use for WHAT we do
Use it for:
- Noir `.nr` work and `Nargo.toml`
- Aztec.nr contract structure, storage layout, notes, nullifiers
- aztec.js integration and TypeScript client usage
- Searching `node_modules/@aztec/` for the exact devnet version behavior

**Hard rule**
Prefer Aztec plugin commands + MCP search over guessing syntax or APIs.


## B2) Session start rule (version alignment)
At the start of a session where Aztec/Noir changes are expected:
- Run `/aztec-version` and align it to the versions in Section A.

If there is any mismatch, stop and resolve it before making code changes.

## B3) Aztec plugin shortcuts (use when relevant)
- New contract: `/aztec:new-contract <Name>`
- Add function: `/aztec:add-function <desc>`
- Add test: `/aztec:add-test <desc>`
- Review: `/aztec:review-contract <path>`
- Deploy: `/aztec:deploy <Contract>`
- Generate client: `/aztec:generate-client <Contract>`

## B4) Local security skills (project-scoped)
These are available as slash commands:

- /audit-context-building: Build system context (assets, trust assumptions, flows).
- /entry-point-analyzer: Enumerate external entry points in Noir/Solidity/TS and what state they can change.
- /spec-to-code-compliance: Map docs/spec statements to code + tests, list gaps.
- /insecure-defaults: Identify unsafe defaults and missing checks (especially around migration and replay protection).
- /sharp-edges: Identify confusing or error-prone interfaces and propose safer patterns.

These skills are read-only by design and should not run long tests automatically.


## B5) Documentation mandate (strict consistency check)
**Every code change requires a docs update in this workspace. No exceptions.**

### Minimum required docs update (every change)
- Add an entry to `docs/DEVLOG.md` containing:
  - What changed (bullet list)
  - Files/areas affected
  - How to verify (exact commands run, or exact commands to run)

### Additional required docs updates (when applicable)
- Setup/start changed → update `README.md` and `docs/ops/testing.md`
- Contract interface changed (public functions, events, externally visible behavior) → update `docs/arch/flows.md` and/or a contract reference doc
- Test approach changed → update `docs/ops/testing.md`
- Security/trust assumptions changed → update `docs/arch/threat-model.md`

### Doc style rules
- Prefer short sections, lists, and exact commands.
- Keep docs in the same repo (no external docs).
- When describing behavior, link to the spec/flow doc where possible.

## B6) Solidity guidelines (only when `.sol` is edited)
- Keep changes minimal and easy to review.
- Never change an external interface (public/external function signatures, events) without updating docs.
- Add or update tests that cover the Solidity behavior change.
- Document Solidity-facing interfaces in `docs/solidity/overview.md` (create if missing).

## B7) End-of-turn checklist (must be satisfied before you stop)
1) Tests
   - Run the relevant commands from Section A.
   - State results and any failures.
2) Docs
   - Confirm `docs/DEVLOG.md` was updated.
   - List any other doc files updated.
3) Diff sanity
   - Confirm changes match the plan/spec.
4) If anything was not verified
   - State exactly what was skipped and why, and what command should be run next.


## Bx) Local workflow commands (no GitHub)
- `/review-pr [range]`: Review local diff like a pull request (defaults to `main..HEAD`).
- `/fix-issue <text-or-path>`: Apply a fix from local text, with fast checks by default.

Additional local security skills:
- `/differential-review`
- `/variant-analysis`
- `/static-analysis`
- `/building-secure-contracts`
- `/property-based-testing`

<content full_path="noir/contracts/migrator/src/migration_note.nr">
use dep::aztec::{
    context::PrivateContext,
    macros::notes::custom_note,
    note::note_interface::NoteHash,
    protocol_types::{
        address::AztecAddress,
        constants::{GENERATOR_INDEX__NOTE_HASH, GENERATOR_INDEX__NOTE_NULLIFIER},
        hash::poseidon2_hash_with_separator,
        traits::{Deserialize, Packable, Serialize, ToField},
    },
};

/// MigrationNote - a note that locks a user's original note for migration.
///
/// Uses #[custom_note] because ownership is determined by the migration public key (mpk),
/// not by an Aztec account address. The note hash intentionally excludes the standard `owner`
/// parameter, simplifying cross-rollup verification (the new rollup doesn't need to know
/// old rollup identities).
#[derive(Deserialize, Eq, Serialize, Packable)]
#[custom_note]
pub struct MigrationNote {
    /// Address of the note creator (typically app contract)
    pub note_creator: AztecAddress,
    /// Migration public key (mpk).
    /// Used for cross-rollup ownership proof - user proves knowledge of migration secret key (msk).
    pub mpk: Field,
    /// Identifier of the destination rollup (prevents cross-rollup replay)
    pub destination_rollup: Field,
    /// Data to migrate (e.g., hash of original note data)
    pub migration_data: Field,
}

impl NoteHash for MigrationNote {
    fn compute_note_hash(
        self,
        _owner: AztecAddress,
        storage_slot: Field,
        randomness: Field,
    ) -> Field {
        // Owner is intentionally excluded - mpk serves as the ownership proof.
        poseidon2_hash_with_separator(
            [
                self.note_creator.to_field(),
                self.mpk,
                self.destination_rollup,
                self.migration_data,
                storage_slot,
                randomness,
            ],
            GENERATOR_INDEX__NOTE_HASH,
        )
    }

    fn compute_nullifier(
        self,
        _context: &mut PrivateContext,
        _owner: AztecAddress,
        note_hash_for_nullification: Field,
    ) -> Field {
        // Trait fallback - not used in the migration flow (which calls
        // MigrationNote::compute_destination_rollup_nullifier with msk directly).
        // Ideally, the msk should be requested from the context.
        //
        // Return a deterministic dummy so PXE note discovery
        // can track the note without crashing.
        poseidon2_hash_with_separator(
            [note_hash_for_nullification],
            GENERATOR_INDEX__NOTE_NULLIFIER,
        )
    }

    unconstrained fn compute_nullifier_unconstrained(
        self,
        _owner: AztecAddress,
        note_hash_for_nullification: Field,
    ) -> Field {
        poseidon2_hash_with_separator(
            [note_hash_for_nullification],
            GENERATOR_INDEX__NOTE_NULLIFIER,
        )
    }
}

impl MigrationNote {
    pub fn new(
        note_creator: AztecAddress,
        mpk: Field,
        destination_rollup: Field,
        migration_data: Field,
    ) -> Self {
        Self { note_creator, mpk, destination_rollup, migration_data }
    }

    /// Computes the migration nullifier. Includes msk (migration secret key) so that
    /// observers cannot link old/new rollup identities by predicting the nullifier from
    /// public note fields.
    pub fn compute_destination_rollup_nullifier(
        note_hash_for_nullification: Field,
        msk: Field,
    ) -> Field {
        poseidon2_hash_with_separator(
            [note_hash_for_nullification, msk],
            GENERATOR_INDEX__NOTE_NULLIFIER,
        )
    }

    unconstrained fn compute_destination_rollup_nullifier_unconstrained(
        note_hash_for_nullification: Field,
        msk: Field,
    ) -> Field {
        poseidon2_hash_with_separator(
            [note_hash_for_nullification, msk],
            GENERATOR_INDEX__NOTE_NULLIFIER,
        )
    }
}

</content>

use aztec::protocol_types::{address::AztecAddress, traits::{Deserialize, Packable, Serialize}};

pub struct L2Actor {
    pub version: Field,
    pub address: AztecAddress,
}

<content full_path="noir/contracts/migrator/src/main.nr">
use aztec::macros::aztec as aztec_contract;

mod migration_note;
pub mod types;
pub use aztec::protocol_types::constants::{ARCHIVE_HEIGHT, NOTE_HASH_TREE_HEIGHT};
pub use migration_note::MigrationNote;

#[aztec_contract]
pub contract Migrator {
    use crate::{migration_note::MigrationNote, types::L2Actor};
    use aztec::{
        macros::{functions::{external, initializer}, storage::storage},
        note::note_interface::NoteHash,
        protocol_types::{
            abis::block_header::BlockHeader,
            address::{AztecAddress, EthAddress},
            constants::{ARCHIVE_HEIGHT, NOTE_HASH_TREE_HEIGHT},
            hash::{compute_siloed_note_hash, compute_unique_note_hash, poseidon2_hash},
            merkle_tree::root::root_from_sibling_path,
            traits::Hash,
        },
        state_vars::{
            map::Map, owned::Owned, private_set::PrivateSet, public_immutable::PublicImmutable,
            public_mutable::PublicMutable,
        },
    };
    use aztec::messages::message_delivery::MessageDelivery;

    #[storage]
    struct Storage<Context> {
        // L1 Migrator address
        l1_migrator: PublicImmutable<EthAddress, Context>,
        // old rollup migrator contract
        old_rollup_migrator: PublicImmutable<L2Actor, Context>,

        // Mapping: proven_block_number -> archive_root
        // Allows users to prove against any registered snapshot
        old_archive_roots: Map<u32, PublicMutable<Field, Context>, Context>,
        // Track the latest registered proven block (for convenience)
        latest_proven_block: PublicMutable<u32, Context>,

        // Migration notes created by users (in old rollup)
        migration_notes: Owned<PrivateSet<MigrationNote, Context>, Context>,
    }

    #[external("public")]
    #[initializer]
    fn constructor(l1_migrator: Option<EthAddress>, old_rollup_migrator: Option<L2Actor>) {
        assert(
            l1_migrator.is_some() == old_rollup_migrator.is_some(),
            "Must provide both L1 migrator and old rollup migrator, or neither",
        );
        if l1_migrator.is_some() {
            self.storage.l1_migrator.initialize(l1_migrator.unwrap());
            self.storage.old_rollup_migrator.initialize(old_rollup_migrator.unwrap());
        }
    }

    // Register old rollup archive root by consuming L1-L2 message from L1Migrator
    // Can be called multiple times to register new snapshots as users create lock notes
    #[external("public")]
    fn register_archive_root(
        archive_root: Field,
        proven_block_number: u32,
        secret: Field,
        leaf_index: Field,
    ) {
        let old_rollup_version = self.storage.old_rollup_migrator.read().version;
        // Verify the L1-L2 message content matches
        // Content was: poseidon2(oldVersion, archiveRoot, provenBlockNumber)
        let content = poseidon2_hash([
            old_rollup_version,
            archive_root,
            proven_block_number as Field,
        ]);

        // Consume L1-L2 message from L1Migrator
        self.context.consume_l1_to_l2_message(
            content,
            secret,
            self.storage.l1_migrator.read(),
            leaf_index,
        );

        // Store archive root indexed by proven block number
        self.storage.old_archive_roots.at(proven_block_number).write(archive_root);

        // Update latest if this is newer
        let current_latest = self.storage.latest_proven_block.read();
        if proven_block_number as u64 > current_latest as u64 {
            self.storage.latest_proven_block.write(proven_block_number);
        }
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Mode A: Routine Migration (on OLD rollup)
    // ============================================================

    #[external("private")]
    fn lock_migration_note(
        note_owner: AztecAddress,
        destination_rollup: Field,
        owner_msk: Field,
        migration_data: Field,
    ) {
        let note_creator = self.context.msg_sender().unwrap();
        let owner_mpk = poseidon2_hash([owner_msk]);
        let migration_note =
            MigrationNote::new(note_creator, owner_mpk, destination_rollup, migration_data);
        self.storage.migration_notes.at(note_owner).insert(migration_note).deliver(
            MessageDelivery.CONSTRAINED_ONCHAIN,
        );
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Mode A: Routine Migration (on NEW rollup)
    // ============================================================
    //
    // User flow:
    // 1. On OLD rollup: User calls app contract to nullify original note and create MigrationNote
    // 2. On NEW rollup: User calls app contract which calls this function to prove the MigrationNote exists
    //
    // MigrationNote structure:
    //   - owner_msk: Point      (migration secret key - for ownership proof)
    //   - migration_data: Field (e.g. hash of original note data)
    //   - destination_rollup: Field (must match current rollup)
    //
    // Verification chain:
    //   migration_note_hash -> (merkle proof) -> note_hash_tree_root
    //       -> (part of) -> block_header
    //           -> (hash to) -> block_header_hash
    //               -> (merkle proof) -> archive_root (trusted from L1)
    #[external("private")]
    fn migrate_mode_a(
        // migration secret key
        msk: Field,
        // MigrationNote fields
        migration_note_creator: AztecAddress,
        migration_data: Field,
        // Lock note hashing data
        migration_note_storage_slot: Field,
        migration_note_randomness: Field,
        // Siloing data
        migration_note_nonce: Field,
        // Note hash tree membership proof
        migration_note_hash_leaf_index: Field,
        migration_note_hash_sibling_path: [Field; NOTE_HASH_TREE_HEIGHT],
        // Full block header (to verify note_hash_tree_root is bound to archive)
        archive_block_header: BlockHeader,
        // Archive membership proof (proves block header hash is in archive)
        archive_leaf_index: Field,
        archive_sibling_path: [Field; ARCHIVE_HEIGHT],
    ) {
        // 0. Verify destination_rollup matches current rollup
        let current_rollup = self.context.version();
        // 1. Verify ownership: caller must know msk corresponding to mpk
        let mpk = poseidon2_hash([msk]);
        // 2. Compute the MigrationNote hash
        //    Owner is ignored by our #[custom_note] - mpk serves as ownership proof
        let migration_note =
            MigrationNote::new(migration_note_creator, mpk, current_rollup, migration_data);
        let migration_note_hash = migration_note.compute_note_hash(
            AztecAddress::zero(),
            migration_note_storage_slot,
            migration_note_randomness,
        );

        // 3. Compute siloed note hash (tied to the old lock contract)
        let siloed_note_hash = compute_siloed_note_hash(
            self.storage.old_rollup_migrator.read().address,
            migration_note_hash,
        );
        // 4. Compute unique note hash (what's actually in the tree)
        let unique_note_hash = compute_unique_note_hash(migration_note_nonce, siloed_note_hash);
        // 5. Extract note_hash_tree_root from block header
        let note_hash_tree_root = archive_block_header.state.partial.note_hash_tree.root;
        // 6. Verify unique_note_hash is in the note_hash_tree
        let computed_note_hash_tree_root = root_from_sibling_path(
            unique_note_hash,
            migration_note_hash_leaf_index,
            migration_note_hash_sibling_path,
        );
        assert(
            computed_note_hash_tree_root == note_hash_tree_root,
            "Lock note not in note hash tree",
        );

        // 7. Compute block header hash
        let archive_block_header_hash = archive_block_header.hash();
        // 8. Compute archive root from merkle proof (verification happens in public part)
        let computed_archive_root = root_from_sibling_path(
            archive_block_header_hash,
            archive_leaf_index,
            archive_sibling_path,
        );

        // 9. Compute and push migration nullifier (prevents double-claiming)
        let migration_nullifier =
            MigrationNote::compute_destination_rollup_nullifier(migration_note_hash, msk);
        self.context.push_nullifier(migration_nullifier);

        // 10. Call public function to verify archive root
        Migrator::at(self.context.this_address())
            .complete_migration(
                archive_block_header.global_variables.block_number,
                computed_archive_root,
            )
            .enqueue(self.context);
    }

    // Verify archive root matches, check destination, and mark note as migrated
    #[external("public")]
    fn complete_migration(archive_block_number: u32, computed_archive_root: Field) {
        // Verify archive root matches the registered one for this block
        let stored_archive_root = self.storage.old_archive_roots.at(archive_block_number).read();
        assert(stored_archive_root != 0, "Archive root not registered for this block");
        assert(
            computed_archive_root == stored_archive_root,
            "Archive root mismatch - note not in old rollup",
        );
    }

    // ============================================================
    // View functions
    // ============================================================

    #[external("utility")]
    unconstrained fn get_old_archive_root(proven_block_number: u32) -> Field {
        self.storage.old_archive_roots.at(proven_block_number).read()
    }

    #[external("utility")]
    unconstrained fn get_latest_proven_block() -> u32 {
        self.storage.latest_proven_block.read()
    }
}

</content>

<content full_path="noir/contracts/example_app/src/main.nr">
use aztec::macros::aztec;

/// Example migration-aware token contract.
///
/// This contract demonstrates how to implement Mode A locking on the OLD rollup.
/// Users call `lock_for_migration()` to:
/// 1. Nullify their original token note
/// 2. Create a MigrationNote that can be proven on the new rollup
#[aztec]
pub contract ExampleMigrationApp {
    use aztec::{
        macros::{functions::{external, initializer}, storage::storage},
        messages::message_delivery::MessageDelivery,
        protocol_types::{
            abis::block_header::BlockHeader, address::AztecAddress, hash::poseidon2_hash,
            traits::Serialize,
        },
        state_vars::{owned::Owned, public_immutable::PublicImmutable},
    };
    use balance_set::balance_set::BalanceSet;
    use migrator::{ARCHIVE_HEIGHT, Migrator, NOTE_HASH_TREE_HEIGHT};

    #[storage]
    struct Storage<Context> {
        old_rollup_app_address: PublicImmutable<AztecAddress, Context>,
        // Token balances (using Aztec's BalanceSet for private balances)
        balances: Owned<BalanceSet<Context>, Context>,
    }

    #[external("public")]
    #[initializer]
    fn constructor(old_rollup_app_address: Option<AztecAddress>) {
        if old_rollup_app_address.is_some() {
            self.storage.old_rollup_app_address.initialize(old_rollup_app_address.unwrap());
        }
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Standard token operations
    // ============================================================

    /// Mint tokens to an account (for testing)
    #[external("private")]
    fn mint(to: AztecAddress, amount: u128) {
        self.storage.balances.at(to).add(amount).deliver(MessageDelivery.CONSTRAINED_ONCHAIN);
    }

    /// Get balance (view function)
    #[external("utility")]
    unconstrained fn get_balance(account: AztecAddress) -> u128 {
        self.storage.balances.at(account).balance_of()
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Mode A: Lock for Migration (on OLD rollup)
    // ============================================================

    /// Lock a token note for migration to a new rollup.
    ///
    /// This function:
    /// 1. Takes a UintNote from the caller's balance
    /// 2. Nullifies the original note (preventing double-spend)
    /// 3. Creates a MigrationNote that can be proven on the destination rollup
    #[external("private")]
    fn lock_for_migration(
        migrator_address: AztecAddress,
        amount: u128,
        destination_rollup: Field,
        owner_msk: Field,
    ) {
        let note_owner = self.context.msg_sender().unwrap();

        // 1. Subtract from balance (this nullifies notes internally)
        //    The BalanceSet handles note selection and nullification
        //    We don't need to deliver since we're locking, not transferring
        let _ = self.storage.balances.at(note_owner).sub(amount);

        // 2. Compute migration data
        let serialized = amount.serialize();
        let migration_data = poseidon2_hash(serialized);

        // 3. Call Migrator contract to create and store the MigrationNote
        let _ = self.call(Migrator::at(migrator_address).lock_migration_note(
            note_owner,
            destination_rollup,
            owner_msk,
            migration_data,
        ));

        // The lock note is now in the note hash tree and can be proven
        // on the new rollup using migrate_via_proof()
    }

    // ============================================================
    // Mode A: Migrate via Proof (on NEW rollup)
    // ============================================================

    #[external("private")]
    fn migrate(
        migrator_address: AztecAddress,
        // migration secret key
        msk: Field,
        // MigrationNote fields
        amount: u128,
        // Lock note hashing data
        migration_note_storage_slot: Field,
        migration_note_randomness: Field,
        // Siloing data
        migration_note_nonce: Field,
        // Note hash tree membership proof
        migration_note_hash_leaf_index: Field,
        migration_note_hash_sibling_path: [Field; NOTE_HASH_TREE_HEIGHT],
        // Full block header (to verify note_hash_tree_root is bound to archive)
        archive_block_header: BlockHeader,
        // Archive membership proof (proves block header hash is in archive)
        archive_leaf_index: Field,
        archive_sibling_path: [Field; ARCHIVE_HEIGHT],
    ) {
        // 1. Compute migration_data (must match what was stored in MigrationNote on old rollup)
        let serialized = amount.serialize();
        let migration_data = poseidon2_hash(serialized);

        // 2. Call Migrator to verify the proof and mark the MigrationNote as migrated
        let migration_note_creator = self.storage.old_rollup_app_address.read();
        let _ = self.call(Migrator::at(migrator_address).migrate_mode_a(
            msk,
            migration_note_creator, // migration_note_creator is the OLD app that called lock_migration_note
            migration_data,
            migration_note_storage_slot,
            migration_note_randomness,
            migration_note_nonce,
            migration_note_hash_leaf_index,
            migration_note_hash_sibling_path,
            archive_block_header,
            archive_leaf_index,
            archive_sibling_path,
        ));

        // 3. If successful, mint the migrated tokens to the user on the new rollup
        self.storage.balances.at(self.context.msg_sender().unwrap()).add(amount).deliver(
            MessageDelivery.CONSTRAINED_ONCHAIN,
        );
    }
}

</content>
